 ● This is a comprehensive unified identity migration plan for the
   eafix-modular repository. It consolidates seven existing spec files
   into a V3 template deliverable for implementing a two-layer identity
   system (physical + semantic).

   Key points:

     - Creates 20-digit numeric IDs for files (1* prefix), directories
   (2* prefix), modules (5* prefix), and process steps (6* prefix)
     - Uses registry-only mode for file IDs (no filename renames)
     - 8 phases with clear gates and validation at each step
     - Final deliverable: unified_identity_migration_plan.json
   following the V3 template structure

   Would you like me to execute this plan by generating the V3 template
   JSON file, or start implementing specific phases?

 > "C:\Users\richg\eafix-modular\✳ Claude Code.txt"Feedback: the plan
   is directionally right, but it still has a few hard problems and a
   couple of places where it over-asserts certainty.

   What it gets right

   The two-layer split is the correct design. Separating physical
   identity (`file_id`, `directory_id`) from semantic identity
   (`module_id`, `process_step_id`) matches the revised plan-change
   notes and avoids mixing filesystem identity with architecture
   identity.

   The decision to make file IDs registry-only is the right one for
   this repo. Your own change notes already reject repo-wide filename
   embedding as too dangerous, and the config schema explicitly
   supports `registry_assigned` with `rename_required: false`. That is
   the safer path for a codebase with many existing imports and
   references.

   The proposed execution order is also right: physical scanner, then
   allocator, then physical validator, then semantic map, then
   generator/validator refactor. That matches the “Immediate next
   steps” file and is the correct dependency chain.

   The plan also fixes a real current weakness: the existing alignment
   report passes overall, but still shows 41 blank `file_id` values and
    189 blank `module_id` values in `file_registry.csv`. So the new
   `physical_status` / `alignment_status` / `readiness_status` split is
    justified.

   Where the plan is weak or incomplete

   The statement that the repo has “~855 files” is not grounded by the
   artifacts you supplied here. The inventory file snippet clearly
   shows many Python files, but I do not see an authoritative repo-wide
    total in the provided materials. Treat that number as provisional
   unless you generate it from the baseline scanner.

   The plan assumes exact `relative_path` joins from
   `physical_id_registry.csv` into `file_registry.csv`. That is correct
    in principle, but it is riskier than the plan admits because your
   current source evidence shows mixed path realities: canonical
   process artifacts, service entrypoints, legacy folders, duplicated
   watcher files, and non-service directories all exist in the repo
   inventory. A straight path join will only work if path normalization
    rules are frozen first.

   The biggest blind spot is that the semantic layer is still cleaner
   than the repo itself. Your process and catalog layer is 28 modules /
    26 steps, but the repo inventory contains many files in shared,
   tests, compliance, contracts, ci, dag, scripts, tools, and
   “Directory management system” areas that do not map cleanly to the
   trading pipeline modules. The plan needs an explicit rule for files
   that are:

   * non-semantic support files
   * cross-cutting shared files
   * legacy/archive files
   * governance/tooling files
   * deliberately unmapped files

   Without that, `readiness_status` will produce noise or force bad
   module assignments. The current warning of 189 blank `module_id`
   values is already evidence of that problem.

   The plan under-specifies the physical registry shape. In one place
   it uses `physical_id_registry.csv` with a single `physical_id`
   column, but the rest of the design distinguishes `file_id` and
   `directory_id`. That is not clean enough. The physical registry
   should either have separate columns for `file_id` and
   `directory_id`, or use `object_type` plus a clearly typed
   `physical_id`. Right now the downstream linkage logic wants separate
    file and directory identities, so separate columns or a formally
   typed schema would be better.

   The `.dir_id` approach is sound, but the plan should explicitly say
   whether hidden directories and legacy folders like `Directory
   management system` are in scope or excluded. Your config list covers
    common technical exclusions, but not awkward repo-internal legacy
   content. That matters because the inventory clearly includes that
   subtree.

   The semantic plan should be stricter about module aliases. The
   current catalog already contains legacy alias modules `O2_OMS` and
   `O3_PNL_CLASSIFIER`, while the process catalog uses
   `O2_OMS_STATE_MACHINE` and `O3_TRADE_CLOSE_CLASSIFIER`. The new
   `identifier_map.json` must treat aliases as metadata only and
   prevent them from surviving as canonical generated module rows
   unless you intentionally keep them as deprecated compatibility
   records.

   The module catalog contract cleanup is only half done. Your strict
   target spec correctly says `invariants` should be top-level instead
   of living under `quality_gates.invariants`, but the current actual
   catalog still puts invariants under `quality_gates` for at least
   some records. The migration plan should explicitly include that
   schema/data reshape, not just numeric ID migration.

   What needs to be added before implementation

   Add a formal path normalization contract.
   You need one rule set for slash direction, root stripping, case
   handling, and duplicate separators before any cross-layer join by
   `relative_path`.

   Add an explicit unmapped-file policy.
   There needs to be a valid state like `module_id = blank +
   classification = out_of_scope_support` or a separate linkage status,
    otherwise the validator will force false failures on files that are
    not part of the 28-module semantic architecture.

   Add a physical registry schema.
   Not just a CSV name. A real contract for columns, uniqueness, parent
    linkage, and one-row-per-object behavior.

   Add object counts as a mandatory gate.
   The baseline scanner must emit counts for:

   * included files
   * excluded files
   * included directories
   * excluded directories
   * files with assigned IDs
   * directories with assigned IDs

   Otherwise “full coverage” is too hand-wavy.

   Add an alias policy.
   State whether deprecated aliases remain as rows in
   `module_catalog.json` or live only inside `identifier_map.json`.
   Right now the materials show both patterns.

   Add a shared/support classification policy.
   The repo clearly has shared libraries and cross-cutting tooling.
   Those need deterministic semantic handling instead of being squeezed
    into pipeline modules.

   Direct verdict

   The plan is mostly correct architecturally and much better than the
   earlier mixed approach. The strongest parts are:

   * physical/semantic separation
   * registry-only file IDs
   * physical-first execution order
   * three-status validator model

   The main remaining problems are:

   * path-join fragility
   * no strong rule for unmapped/support/legacy files
   * incomplete alias policy
   * incomplete physical registry contract
   * a few claims that are more assumed than proven

   So: good foundation, not ready to execute unchanged.

   The next correction I would make is this:

   Make `PH-01` produce a mandatory classification baseline with these
   columns in addition to raw inventory:

   * `object_scope_class`
   * `candidate_semantic_role`
   * `path_normalized`
   * `is_semantic_candidate`

   That will expose how much of the repo can actually participate in
   semantic migration before you touch the generator.

 ● I'll create a revised plan that addresses the identified weaknesses
   and adds the missing contracts and policies.

     10 +EXPECTED_FILE_PATTERN = r"^1\d{19}$"
     11 +EXPECTED_DIRECTORY_PATTERN = r"^2\d{19}$"
     12 +REQUIRED_BOOTSTRAP_FILES = (
     13 +    "COUNTER_STORE.json",
     14 +    "id_migration/config/path_normalization_rules.json",
     15 +    "id_migration/config/file_classification_rules.json",

     17 +    "id_migration/schemas/physical_id_registry.schema.json",
     18 +)

     20 +
     21 +def load_json(path: Path) -> Any:
     22 +    with path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as handle:
     23 +        return json.load(handle)
     24 +
     25 +
     26 +def fail(message: str) -> int:
     27 +    print(message, file=sys.stderr)
     28 +    return 1
     29 +
     30 +
     31 +def validate_manual(config: dict[str, Any], repo_root: Path) ->
          list[str]:
     32 +    errors: list[str] = []
     33 +    required_keys = {
     34 +        "repository_root",
     35 +        "excluded_directories",
     36 +        "excluded_files",
     37 +        "assign_root_directory_id",
     38 +        "directory_identity_mechanism",
     39 +        "file_identity_mechanism",
     40 +        "physical_id_patterns",
     41 +    }
     42 +
     43 +    if set(config) != required_keys:
     44 +        missing = sorted(required_keys - set(config))
     45 +        extra = sorted(set(config) - required_keys)
     46 +        if missing:
     47 +            errors.append(f"missing required keys: {', '.join(m
         issing)}")
     48 +        if extra:
     49 +            errors.append(f"unexpected keys: {', '.join(extra)}
         ")
     50 +
     51 +    repository_root = Path(str(config.get("repository_root", ""
         )))
     52 +    if not repository_root.is_absolute():
     53 +        errors.append("repository_root must be an absolute path
         ")
     54 +    elif repository_root.resolve() != repo_root.resolve():
     55 +        errors.append(
     56 +            f"repository_root must resolve to {repo_root}, got
         {repository_root.resolve()}"
     57 +        )
     58 +
     59 +    for key in ("excluded_directories", "excluded_files"):
     60 +        value = config.get(key)
     61 +        if not isinstance(value, list) or not all(isinstance(it
         em, str) for item in value):
     62 +            errors.append(f"{key} must be a list of strings")
     63 +        elif len(value) != len(set(value)):
     64 +            errors.append(f"{key} contains duplicate entries")
     65 +
     66 +    if not isinstance(config.get("assign_root_directory_id"), b
         ool):
     67 +        errors.append("assign_root_directory_id must be boolean
         ")
     68 +
     69 +    directory_mechanism = config.get("directory_identity_mechan
         ism")
     70 +    if not isinstance(directory_mechanism, dict):
     71 +        errors.append("directory_identity_mechanism must be an
         object")
     72 +    else:
     73 +        if directory_mechanism.get("mechanism") != "sidecar_anc
         hor_file":
     74 +            errors.append("directory_identity_mechanism.mechani
         sm must be sidecar_anchor_file")
     75 +        if directory_mechanism.get("anchor_filename") != ".dir_
         id":
     76 +            errors.append("directory_identity_mechanism.anchor_
         filename must be .dir_id")
     77 +        if not isinstance(directory_mechanism.get("anchor_requi
         red"), bool):
     78 +            errors.append("directory_identity_mechanism.anchor_
         required must be boolean")
     79 +
     80 +    file_mechanism = config.get("file_identity_mechanism")
     81 +    if not isinstance(file_mechanism, dict):
     82 +        errors.append("file_identity_mechanism must be an objec
         t")
     83 +    else:
     84 +        if file_mechanism.get("mechanism") != "registry_assigne
         d":
     85 +            errors.append("file_identity_mechanism.mechanism mu
         st be registry_assigned")
     86 +        if file_mechanism.get("rename_required") is not False:
     87 +            errors.append("file_identity_mechanism.rename_requi
         red must be false")
     88 +
     89 +    patterns = config.get("physical_id_patterns")
     90 +    if not isinstance(patterns, dict):
     91 +        errors.append("physical_id_patterns must be an object")
     92 +    else:
     93 +        if patterns.get("id_length") != 20:
     94 +            errors.append("physical_id_patterns.id_length must
         be 20")
     95 +        if patterns.get("file_id_pattern") != EXPECTED_FILE_PAT
         TERN:
     96 +            errors.append(
     97 +                "physical_id_patterns.file_id_pattern must be t
         he literal regex ^1\\d{19}$"
     98 +            )
     99 +        if patterns.get("directory_id_pattern") != EXPECTED_DIR
         ECTORY_PATTERN:
    100 +            errors.append(
    101 +                "physical_id_patterns.directory_id_pattern must
          be the literal regex ^2\\d{19}$"
    102 +            )
    103 +
    104 +    return errors
    105 +
    106 +
    107 +def validate_schema(config: dict[str, Any], schema: dict[str, A
         ny]) -> list[str]:
    108 +    try:
    109 +        from jsonschema import Draft202012Validator
    110 +    except ImportError:
    111 +        return []
    112 +
    113 +    validator = Draft202012Validator(schema)
    114 +    return [error.message for error in validator.iter_errors(co
         nfig)]
    115 +
    116 +
    117 +def validate_bootstrap_files(repo_root: Path) -> list[str]:
    118 +    errors: list[str] = []
    119 +    for relative_path in REQUIRED_BOOTSTRAP_FILES:
    120 +        full_path = repo_root / relative_path
    121 +        if not full_path.is_file():
    122 +            errors.append(f"required bootstrap file missing: {r
         elative_path}")
    123 +            continue
    124 +        try:
    125 +            load_json(full_path)
    126 +        except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
    127 +            errors.append(f"invalid JSON in {relative_path}: {e
         xc}")
    128 +    return errors
    129 +
    130 +
    131 +def main(argv: list[str]) -> int:
    132 +    if len(argv) != 2:
    133 +        return fail(
    134 +            "usage: python id_migration/scripts/validate_physic
         al_id_config.py "
    135 +            "id_migration/config/physical_id_config.json"
    136 +        )
    137 +
    138 +    repo_root = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]
    139 +    schema_path = repo_root / "EA-REG" / "physical_id_config_sc
         hema.json"
    140 +    config_path = (repo_root / argv[1]).resolve()
    141 +
    142 +    if not schema_path.is_file():
    143 +        return fail(f"schema not found: {schema_path}")
    144 +    if not config_path.is_file():
    145 +        return fail(f"config not found: {config_path}")
    146 +
    147 +    try:
    148 +        schema = load_json(schema_path)
    149 +        config = load_json(config_path)
    150 +    except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
    151 +        return fail(f"invalid JSON: {exc}")
    152 +
    156 +    errors = []
    157 +    errors.extend(validate_schema(config, schema))
    158 +    errors.extend(validate_manual(config, repo_root))
    159 +    errors.extend(validate_bootstrap_files(repo_root))
    160 +
    161 +    if errors:
    162 +        print("physical_id_config validation failed:", file=sys
         .stderr)
    163 +        for error in errors:
    164 +            print(f"- {error}", file=sys.stderr)
    165 +        return 1
    166 +
    167 +    print("physical_id_config.json validated successfully")
    168 +    return 0
    169 +
    170 +
    171 +if __name__ == "__main__":
    172 +    raise SystemExit(main(sys.argv))

─ Worked for 1m 22s ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

• There’s one important design gap in the spec: file IDs are supposed to
  be registry_assigned with rename_required=false, but the registry is
  also described as derived-only. That means file ID persistence has to
  live somewhere else, so I’m using the migration manifest as the
  allocation ledger for files and keeping .dir_id as the directory
  source of truth.

    192 +def build_assignment_plan(
    193 +    rows: list[dict[str, str]],
    194 +    config: dict[str, Any],
    195 +    counter_store: dict[str, Any],
    196 +    existing_file_assignments: dict[str, dict[str, str]],
    197 +    existing_directory_ids: dict[str, dict[str, str]],

    203 +    directory_actions: list[dict[str, Any]] = []

    215 +    )

    218 +        if as_bool(row["is_excluded"]):

         chor_name

    223 +        if existing:
    224 +            directory_id = existing["directory_id"]
    225 +            status = "preserved"
    226 +            preserved_ids += 1
    227 +        else:
    228 +            directory_id = allocate_next_id(plan_counter_store,
          "directory_id", DIRECTORY_ID_PREFIX)
    229 +            status = "assigned"
    230 +            new_allocations += 1
    231 +
    232 +        directory_actions.append(
    233 +            {
    234 +                "relative_path": relative_path,
    235 +                "anchor_path": anchor_path,
    236 +                "directory_id": directory_id,
    237 +                "status": status,
    238 +            }
    239 +        )
    240 +
    241 +    for row in file_rows:
    242 +        if as_bool(row["is_excluded"]):
    243 +            continue
    244 +        relative_path = row["relative_path"]
    245 +        existing = existing_file_assignments.get(relative_path)
    246 +        if existing:
    247 +            file_id = existing["file_id"]
    248 +            status = "preserved"
    249 +            preserved_ids += 1

    251 +            file_id = allocate_next_id(plan_counter_store, "fil
         e_id", FILE_ID_PREFIX)
    252 +            status = "assigned"
    253 +            new_allocations += 1
    254 +
    255 +        file_actions.append(
    256 +            {
    257 +                "relative_path": relative_path,
    258 +                "file_id": file_id,
    259 +                "status": status,
    260 +            }
    261 +        )
    262 +
    263 +    return {
    264 +        "counter_store_after": plan_counter_store,
    265 +        "directories": directory_actions,
    266 +        "files": file_actions,
    267 +        "counts": {
    268 +            "directories_with_directory_id": len(directory_acti
         ons),
    269 +            "files_with_file_id": len(file_actions),
    270 +            "new_allocations": new_allocations,
    271 +            "preserved_ids": preserved_ids,
    272 +        },
    273 +    }
    274 +
    275 +
    276 +def make_manifest_events(
    277 +    mode: str,
    278 +    run_id: str,
    279 +    directory_actions: list[dict[str, Any]],
    280 +    file_actions: list[dict[str, Any]],
    281 +) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
    282 +    emitted_at = utc_now()
    283 +    events: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
    284 +
    285 +    for index, action in enumerate(directory_actions, start=1):
    286 +        events.append(
    287 +            {
    288 +                "run_id": run_id,
    289 +                "emitted_at_utc": emitted_at,
    290 +                "mode": mode,
    291 +                "sequence": index,
    292 +                "event_type": DIRECTORY_EVENT_TYPES[mode],
    293 +                "object_type": "directory",
    294 +                "relative_path": action["relative_path"],
    295 +                "directory_id": action["directory_id"],
    296 +                "status": action["status"],
    297 +                "anchor_filename": ".dir_id",
    298 +                "anchor_path": str(action["anchor_path"].relati
         ve_to(REPO_ROOT)).replace("\\", "/"),
    299 +            }
    300 +        )
    301 +
    302 +    base_sequence = len(events)
    303 +    for index, action in enumerate(file_actions, start=1):
    304 +        events.append(
    305 +            {
    306 +                "run_id": run_id,
    307 +                "emitted_at_utc": emitted_at,
    308 +                "mode": mode,
    309 +                "sequence": base_sequence + index,
    310 +                "event_type": FILE_EVENT_TYPES[mode],
    311 +                "object_type": "file",
    312 +                "relative_path": action["relative_path"],
    313 +                "new_relative_path": action["relative_path"],
    314 +                "file_id": action["file_id"],
    315 +                "status": action["status"],
    316 +                "rename_required": False,
    317 +                "note": "registry_assigned_no_filename_change",
    318 +            }
    319 +        )
    320 +
    321 +    return events
    322 +
    323 +
    324 +def write_dir_anchor(anchor_path: Path, directory_id: str, rela
         tive_path: str, project_root_id: str | None) -> None:
    325 +    payload = {
    326 +        "dir_id": directory_id,
    327 +        "allocated_at_utc": utc_now(),
    328 +        "allocator_version": ALLOCATOR_VERSION,
    329 +        "project_root_id": project_root_id,
    330 +        "relative_path": relative_path,
    331 +    }
    332 +    anchor_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    333 +    with anchor_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")
         as handle:
    334 +        json.dump(payload, handle, indent=2)
    335 +        handle.write("\n")
    336 +
    337 +
    338 +def run_plan(
    339 +    plan: dict[str, Any],
    340 +    manifest_path: Path,
    341 +) -> None:
    342 +    run_id = f"plan_{datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime('%Y%m%
         dT%H%M%SZ')}"
    343 +    events = make_manifest_events("plan", run_id, plan["directo
         ries"], plan["files"])
    344 +    append_jsonl(manifest_path, events)
    345 +    print(json.dumps(plan["counts"], indent=2))
    346 +    print(f"Manifest appended: {manifest_path}")
    347 +
    348 +
    349 +def run_apply(
    350 +    plan: dict[str, Any],
    351 +    counter_store_path: Path,
    352 +    manifest_path: Path,
    353 +    assign_root_directory_id: bool,
    354 +) -> None:
    355 +    counter_store_after = plan["counter_store_after"]
    356 +    counters_changed = plan["counts"]["new_allocations"] > 0
    357 +    if counters_changed:
    358 +        counter_store_after["last_updated_utc"] = utc_now()
    359 +        write_json_atomic(counter_store_path, counter_store_aft
         er)
    360 +
    361 +    project_root_id = None if not assign_root_directory_id else
          counter_store_after["counters"]["directory_id"]
    362 +    for action in plan["directories"]:
    363 +        if action["status"] != "assigned":
    364 +            continue
    365 +        write_dir_anchor(action["anchor_path"], action["directo
         ry_id"], action["relative_path"], project_root_id)
    366 +
    367 +    run_id = f"apply_{datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime('%Y%m
         %dT%H%M%SZ')}"
    368 +    events = make_manifest_events("apply", run_id, plan["direct
         ories"], plan["files"])
    369 +    append_jsonl(manifest_path, events)
    370 +
    371 +    print(json.dumps(plan["counts"], indent=2))
    372 +    if counters_changed:
    373 +        print(f"Updated counter store: {counter_store_path}")
    374 +    print(f"Manifest appended: {manifest_path}")
    375 +
    376 +
    377 +def derive_registry(
    378 +    rows: list[dict[str, str]],
    379 +    config: dict[str, Any],
    380 +    manifest_path: Path,
    381 +    registry_path: Path,
    382 +) -> dict[str, int]:
    383 +    anchor_name = config["directory_identity_mechanism"]["ancho
         r_filename"]
    384 +    existing_file_assignments = load_existing_file_assignments(
         manifest_path, registry_path)
    385 +    directory_state = scan_existing_directory_ids(rows, anchor_
         name)
    386 +
    387 +    registry_rows: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
    388 +    missing_paths: list[str] = []
    389 +
    390 +    for row in rows:
    391 +        is_excluded = as_bool(row["is_excluded"])
    392 +        exists_on_disk = as_bool(row["exists_on_disk"])
    393 +        relative_path = row["relative_path"]
    394 +        parent_relative_path = row["parent_relative_path"]
    395 +        parent_directory_id = ""
    396 +        if parent_relative_path:
    397 +            parent_directory_id = directory_state.get(parent_re
         lative_path, {}).get("directory_id", "")
    398 +
    399 +        record = {
    400 +            "object_type": row["object_type"],
    401 +            "file_id": "",
    402 +            "directory_id": "",
    403 +            "relative_path": relative_path,
    404 +            "name": row["name"],
    405 +            "parent_relative_path": parent_relative_path,
    406 +            "parent_directory_id": parent_directory_id,
    407 +            "extension": row["extension"] if row["object_type"]
          == "file" else "",
    408 +            "id_source": "preserved",
    409 +            "is_excluded": is_excluded,
    410 +            "exists_on_disk": exists_on_disk,
    411 +        }
    412 +
    413 +        if row["object_type"] == "directory":
    414 +            if not is_excluded:
    415 +                directory_id = directory_state.get(relative_pat
         h, {}).get("directory_id", "")
    416 +                if not directory_id:
    417 +                    missing_paths.append(relative_path)
    418 +                record["directory_id"] = directory_id
    419 +                status = directory_state.get(relative_path, {})
         .get("status", "preserved")
    420 +                record["id_source"] = "COUNTER_STORE" if status
          == "assigned" else "preserved"
    421 +        else:
    422 +            if not is_excluded:
    423 +                file_assignment = existing_file_assignments.get
         (relative_path)
    424 +                if not file_assignment:
    425 +                    missing_paths.append(relative_path)
    426 +                else:
    427 +                    record["file_id"] = file_assignment["file_i
         d"]
    428 +                    record["id_source"] = "COUNTER_STORE" if fi
         le_assignment["status"] == "assigned" else "preserved"
    429 +
    430 +        registry_rows.append(record)
    431 +
    432 +    if missing_paths:
    433 +        sample = ", ".join(missing_paths[:10])
    434 +        raise RuntimeError(f"missing physical IDs for {len(miss
         ing_paths)} baseline rows: {sample}")
    435 +
    436 +    registry_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    437 +    with registry_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8", newline="")
         as handle:
    438 +        writer = csv.DictWriter(handle, fieldnames=REGISTRY_COL
         UMNS)
    439 +        writer.writeheader()
    440 +        writer.writerows(registry_rows)
    441 +
    442 +    counts = {
    443 +        "files_with_file_id": sum(1 for row in registry_rows if
          row["object_type"] == "file" and row["file_id"]),
    444 +        "directories_with_directory_id": sum(
    445 +            1 for row in registry_rows if row["object_type"] ==
          "directory" and row["directory_id"]
    446 +        ),
    447 +        "total_rows": len(registry_rows),
    448 +    }
    449 +    print(json.dumps(counts, indent=2))
    450 +    print(f"Registry written: {registry_path}")
    451 +    return counts
    452 +
    453 +
    454 +def parse_args(argv: list[str]) -> argparse.Namespace:
    455 +    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="PH-02 physica
         l ID assignment and registry derivation")
    456 +    parser.add_argument("--config", default=str(DEFAULT_CONFIG_
         PATH), help="Path to physical_id_config.json")
    457 +    parser.add_argument("--mode", choices=["plan", "apply", "de
         rive-registry"], help="Execution mode")
    458 +    parser.add_argument(
    459 +        "--derive-registry",
    460 +        action="store_true",
    461 +        help="Alias for --mode derive-registry",
    462 +    )
    463 +    return parser.parse_args(argv)
    464 +
    465 +
    466 +def main(argv: list[str]) -> int:
    467 +    args = parse_args(argv)
    468 +    mode = "derive-registry" if args.derive_registry else args.
         mode
    469 +    if mode is None:
    470 +        print("ERROR: specify --mode {plan,apply,derive-registr
         y} or --derive-registry", file=sys.stderr)
    471 +        return 2
    472 +
    473 +    config_path = Path(args.config)
    474 +    if not config_path.is_absolute():
    475 +        config_path = (REPO_ROOT / config_path).resolve()
    476 +
    477 +    if not config_path.is_file():
    478 +        print(f"ERROR: config not found: {config_path}", file=s
         ys.stderr)
    479 +        return 2
    480 +    if not DEFAULT_BASELINE_PATH.is_file():
    481 +        print(f"ERROR: baseline CSV not found: {DEFAULT_BASELIN
         E_PATH}", file=sys.stderr)
    482 +        return 2
    483 +    if not DEFAULT_COUNTER_STORE_PATH.is_file():
    484 +        print(f"ERROR: counter store not found: {DEFAULT_COUNTE
         R_STORE_PATH}", file=sys.stderr)
    485 +        return 2
    486 +
    487 +    config = load_json(config_path)
    488 +    rows = load_baseline_rows(DEFAULT_BASELINE_PATH)
    489 +
    490 +    if mode == "derive-registry":
    491 +        try:
    492 +            derive_registry(rows, config, DEFAULT_MANIFEST_PATH
         , DEFAULT_REGISTRY_PATH)
    493 +        except Exception as exc:  # pragma: no cover - command-
         line path
    494 +            print(f"ERROR: {exc}", file=sys.stderr)
    495 +            return 1
    496 +        return 0
    497 +
    498 +    try:
    499 +        counter_store = load_counter_store(DEFAULT_COUNTER_STOR
         E_PATH)
    500 +        existing_file_assignments = load_existing_file_assignme
         nts(DEFAULT_MANIFEST_PATH, DEFAULT_REGISTRY_PATH)
    501 +        existing_directory_ids = scan_existing_directory_ids(
    502 +            rows,
    503 +            config["directory_identity_mechanism"]["anchor_file
         name"],
    504 +        )
    505 +        plan = build_assignment_plan(rows, config, counter_stor
         e, existing_file_assignments, existing_directory_ids)
    506 +        if mode == "plan":
    507 +            run_plan(plan, DEFAULT_MANIFEST_PATH)
    508 +        else:
    509 +            run_apply(plan, DEFAULT_COUNTER_STORE_PATH, DEFAULT
         _MANIFEST_PATH, config["assign_root_directory_id"])
    510 +    except Exception as exc:  # pragma: no cover - command-line
          path
    511 +        print(f"ERROR: {exc}", file=sys.stderr)
    512 +        return 1
    513 +
    514 +    return 0
    515 +
    516 +
    517 +if __name__ == "__main__":

• PH-02 is in place.

  I added 02_assign_physical_ids.py and 00_run_migration.py, then ran
  the phase end to end. The allocator uses migration_manifest.jsonl as
  the durable file-ID ledger so file IDs remain stable while filenames
  stay unchanged, which is the only way to reconcile the spec’s
  registry_assigned + rename_required=false rule with a derived
  registry.

  Verification passed:

  - Plan run before apply: 250 directory IDs, 791 file IDs, 1041 new
    allocations.
  - Apply run: created 250 .dir_id anchors and updated
    COUNTER_STORE.json to next IDs 10000000000000000791 and
    20000000000000000250.
  - Derive step wrote physical_id_registry.csv with 1042 rows.
  - Post-apply plan rerun was idempotent: new_allocations: 0,
    preserved_ids: 1041.
  - Registry check: blank_non_excluded: 0, excluded_blank: 1.

  The concrete PH-02 outputs now exist:

  - migration_manifest.jsonl
  - physical_id_registry.csv
  - 250 .dir_id files across governed directories
  - updated COUNTER_STORE.json

  and the new .dir_id files add a large tracked/untracked surface on top
  of that. I did not touch the unrelated deletions/modifications already
  present.

  physical validation gate.

─ Worked for 1m 44s ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

• The main constraint is that PH-02 derives the registry from the pre-anchor baseline, so PH-03 cannot
  naively require every current file on disk to have a registry row; that would incorrectly fail
  on .dir_id, the manifest, and the report itself. I’m implementing the hard gate around the durable
  contract instead:

  1. Validate physical_id_registry.csv header, row typing, ID patterns, normalization, and cross-row
     linkage.
  2. Validate every on-disk .dir_id anchor against schema and ensure each anchor matches a registry
     directory row.
  3. Verify every governed on-disk directory has exactly one valid anchor and that registry
     exists_on_disk rows still exist.
  4. Write id_migration/output/physical_validation_report.json, then run G-02 and inspect any failures
     before reporting back.

     43 +def utc_now() -> str:
     44 +    return datetime.now(timezone.utc).replace(microsecond=0).isoformat().replace("+00:00", "Z
         ")

     47 +def load_json(path: Path) -> Any:
     48 +    with path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as handle:
     49 +        return json.load(handle)
     50 +
     51 +
     52 +def write_json(path: Path, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
     53 +    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
     54 +    with path.open("w", encoding="utf-8", newline="\n") as handle:
     55 +        json.dump(payload, handle, indent=2)
     56 +        handle.write("\n")

     59 +def normalize_relative_path(path_value: str) -> str:
     60 +    value = str(path_value).replace("\\", "/")
     61 +    while value.startswith("./"):
     62 +        value = value[2:]
     63 +    value = re.sub(r"/+", "/", value)
     64 +    value = value.rstrip("/")
     65 +    if value in {"", "."}:
     66 +        return ""
     67 +
     68 +    parts: list[str] = []
     69 +    for segment in value.split("/"):
     70 +        if segment in {"", "."}:
     71 +            continue
     72 +        if segment == "..":
     73 +            if parts:
     74 +                parts.pop()
     75 +            continue
     76 +        parts.append(segment)
     77 +    return "/".join(parts)
     78 +
     79 +
     80 +def normalize_absolute_path(path: Path, repo_root: Path) -> str:
     81 +    return normalize_relative_path(os.path.relpath(path, repo_root))
     82 +
     83 +
     84 +def path_key(path_value: str) -> str:
     85 +    normalized = normalize_relative_path(path_value)
     86 +    return normalized.casefold() if os.name == "nt" else normalized
     87 +
     88 +
     89 +def parse_bool(value: str, *, field: str, line_number: int, errors: list[dict[str, Any]]) ->
         bool:
     90 +    if value == "True":
     91 +        return True
     92 +    if value == "False":
     93 +        return False
     94 +    errors.append(
     95 +        issue(
     96 +            "INVALID_BOOLEAN",
     97 +            f"{field} must be True or False, got {value!r}",
     98 +            line_number=line_number,
     99 +            field=field,
    100 +        )
    101 +    )
    102 +    return False
    103 +
    104 +
    105 +def parse_datetime(value: Any) -> bool:
    106 +    if not isinstance(value, str):
    107 +        return False
    108 +    candidate = value.replace("Z", "+00:00")
    109 +    try:
    110 +        datetime.fromisoformat(candidate)
    111 +    except ValueError:
    112 +        return False
    113 +    return True
    114 +
    115 +
    116 +def issue(
    117 +    code: str,

    121 +    relative_path: str | None = None,
    122 +    field: str | None = None,

    124 +    payload: dict[str, Any] = {"code": code, "message": message}
    125 +    if line_number is not None:
    126 +        payload["line_number"] = line_number
    127 +    if relative_path is not None:
    128 +        payload["relative_path"] = relative_path
    129 +    if field is not None:
    130 +        payload["field"] = field
    131 +    return payload

    134 +def load_classification_rules(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
    135 +    payload = load_json(path)
    136 +    if not isinstance(payload, dict):
    137 +        raise ValueError(f"classification rules must be a JSON object: {path}")
    138 +    return payload
    139 +
    140 +
    141 +def classify_path(rel_path: str, object_type: str, rules_data: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, A
         ny]:
    142 +    default_class = rules_data.get("default_scope_class", "module_owned")
    143 +    classifications = rules_data.get("classifications", {})
    144 +    rules = rules_data.get("rules", [])
    145 +
    146 +    scope_class = default_class
    147 +    match_path = rel_path.replace("\\", "/")
    148 +    match_path_for_rules = f"{match_path}/" if object_type == "directory" and not match_path.
         endswith("/") else match_path
    149 +
    150 +    for rule in rules:
    151 +        match_type = rule.get("match_type")
    152 +        values = rule.get("values", [])
    153 +        matched = False
    154 +        if match_type == "path_prefix":
    155 +            matched = any(match_path_for_rules.startswith(value) or match_path.startswith(val
         ue) for value in values)
    156 +        elif match_type == "path_contains":
    157 +            matched = any(value in match_path_for_rules or value in match_path for value in v
         alues)
    158 +        if matched:
    159 +            scope_class = str(rule.get("scope_class", scope_class))
    160 +            break
    161 +
    162 +    return classifications.get(scope_class, {"object_scope_class": scope_class}) | {"object_s
         cope_class": scope_class}
    163 +
    164 +
    165 +def discover_governed_directories(
    166 +    repo_root: Path,
    167 +    config: dict[str, Any],
    168 +    classification_rules: dict[str, Any],
    169 +) -> set[str]:
    170 +    excluded_dirs = set(config.get("excluded_directories", []))
    171 +    governed_dirs: set[str] = set()
    172 +
    173 +    for dirpath, dirnames, _filenames in os.walk(repo_root, followlinks=False):
    174 +        dir_path = Path(dirpath)
    175 +        rel_dir = normalize_absolute_path(dir_path, repo_root)
    176 +        dir_name = dir_path.name
    177 +
    178 +        if rel_dir:
    179 +            dir_excluded = dir_name in excluded_dirs
    180 +            dir_scope = classify_path(rel_dir, "directory", classification_rules).get("object
         _scope_class")
    181 +            if not dir_excluded and dir_scope != "out_of_scope":
    182 +                governed_dirs.add(rel_dir)
    183 +
    184 +        dirnames[:] = [name for name in dirnames if name not in excluded_dirs]
    185 +
    186 +    return governed_dirs

    189 +def validate_dir_anchor_payload(
    190 +    payload: Any,
    191 +    *,
    192 +    expected_relative_path: str,
    193 +    schema: dict[str, Any] | None,
    194 +) -> list[str]:
    195 +    errors: list[str] = []
    196 +
    197 +    if schema is not None:
    198 +        try:
    199 +            from jsonschema import Draft202012Validator
    200 +        except ImportError:
    201 +            schema = None
    202 +        else:
    203 +            validator = Draft202012Validator(schema)
    204 +            errors.extend(error.message for error in validator.iter_errors(payload))
    205 +
    206 +    if not isinstance(payload, dict):
    207 +        return errors + ["anchor payload must be a JSON object"]
    208 +
    209 +    required_keys = {
    210 +        "dir_id",
    211 +        "allocated_at_utc",
    212 +        "allocator_version",
    213 +        "project_root_id",
    214 +        "relative_path",
    215 +    }
    216 +    if set(payload) != required_keys:
    217 +        missing = sorted(required_keys - set(payload))
    218 +        extra = sorted(set(payload) - required_keys)
    219 +        if missing:
    220 +            errors.append(f"missing keys: {', '.join(missing)}")
    221 +        if extra:
    222 +            errors.append(f"unexpected keys: {', '.join(extra)}")
    223 +
    224 +    dir_id = payload.get("dir_id")
    225 +    if not isinstance(dir_id, str) or not DIRECTORY_ID_PATTERN.fullmatch(dir_id):
    226 +        errors.append("dir_id must match ^2\\d{19}$")
    227 +
    228 +    allocated_at = payload.get("allocated_at_utc")
    229 +    if not parse_datetime(allocated_at):
    230 +        errors.append("allocated_at_utc must be an ISO-8601 datetime")
    231 +
    232 +    allocator_version = payload.get("allocator_version")
    233 +    if not isinstance(allocator_version, str) or not allocator_version.strip():
    234 +        errors.append("allocator_version must be a non-empty string")
    235 +
    236 +    project_root_id = payload.get("project_root_id")
    237 +    if project_root_id is not None and (
    238 +        not isinstance(project_root_id, str) or not DIRECTORY_ID_PATTERN.fullmatch(project_ro
         ot_id)
    239 +    ):
    240 +        errors.append("project_root_id must be null or match ^2\\d{19}$")
    241 +
    242 +    relative_path = payload.get("relative_path")
    243 +    if not isinstance(relative_path, str) or not relative_path:
    244 +        errors.append("relative_path must be a non-empty string")
    245 +    else:
    246 +        normalized = normalize_relative_path(relative_path)
    247 +        if normalized != relative_path:
    248 +            errors.append("relative_path must already be normalized")
    249 +        if not PATH_PATTERN.fullmatch(relative_path):
    250 +            errors.append("relative_path does not satisfy the path normalization contract")
    251 +        if relative_path != expected_relative_path:
    252 +            errors.append(
    253 +                f"relative_path {relative_path!r} does not match anchor location {expected_re
         lative_path!r}"
    254 +            )
    255 +
    256 +    return errors
    257 +

    259 +def load_registry_rows(path: Path) -> tuple[list[dict[str, Any]], list[dict[str, Any]], list[
         dict[str, Any]]]:
    260 +    errors: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
    261 +    warnings: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
    262 +    typed_rows: list[dict[str, Any]] = []

         ine_number))

    283 +            parent_relative_path = row["parent_relative_path"]
    284 +            file_id = row["file_id"]
    285 +            directory_id = row["directory_id"]
    286 +            parent_directory_id = row["parent_directory_id"]

    290 +                row["exists_on_disk"],
    291 +                field="exists_on_disk",
    292 +                line_number=line_number,
    293 +                errors=errors,
    294 +            )
    295 +
    296 +            if object_type not in VALID_OBJECT_TYPES:
    297 +                errors.append(

    299 +                        "INVALID_OBJECT_TYPE",

         t_type!r}",

    303 +                        field="object_type",
    304 +                    )
    305 +                )

    308 +            if normalized_relative_path != relative_path:
    309 +                errors.append(
    310 +                    issue(
    311 +                        "NON_NORMALIZED_PATH",
    312 +                        "relative_path must already be normalized",
    313 +                        line_number=line_number,
    314 +                        relative_path=relative_path or None,
    315 +                        field="relative_path",
    316 +                    )
    317 +                )
    318 +            elif relative_path and not PATH_PATTERN.fullmatch(relative_path):
    319 +                errors.append(
    320 +                    issue(
    321 +                        "INVALID_RELATIVE_PATH",
    322 +                        "relative_path does not satisfy the path normalization contract",
    323 +                        line_number=line_number,
    324 +                        relative_path=relative_path,
    325 +                        field="relative_path",
    326 +                    )
    327 +                )
    328 +
    329 +            normalized_parent_path = normalize_relative_path(parent_relative_path)
    330 +            if normalized_parent_path != parent_relative_path:
    331 +                errors.append(
    332 +                    issue(
    333 +                        "NON_NORMALIZED_PARENT_PATH",
    334 +                        "parent_relative_path must already be normalized",
    335 +                        line_number=line_number,
    336 +                        relative_path=relative_path or None,
    337 +                        field="parent_relative_path",
    338 +                    )
    339 +                )
    340 +            elif parent_relative_path and not PATH_PATTERN.fullmatch(parent_relative_path):
    341 +                errors.append(
    342 +                    issue(
    343 +                        "INVALID_PARENT_PATH",
    344 +                        "parent_relative_path does not satisfy the path normalization contrac
         t",
    345 +                        line_number=line_number,
    346 +                        relative_path=relative_path or None,
    347 +                        field="parent_relative_path",
    348 +                    )
    349 +                )
    350 +
    351 +            if not relative_path:
    352 +                errors.append(issue("MISSING_RELATIVE_PATH", "relative_path must be non-empty
         ", line_number=line_number))
    353 +
    354 +            name = row["name"]
    355 +            expected_name = PurePosixPath(relative_path).name if relative_path else ""
    356 +            if not name:
    357 +                errors.append(issue("MISSING_NAME", "name must be non-empty", line_number=lin
         e_number))
    358 +            elif not NAME_PATTERN.fullmatch(name):
    359 +                errors.append(
    360 +                    issue(

    362 +                        "name must be a basename with no path separators",
    363 +                        line_number=line_number,
    364 +                        relative_path=relative_path or None,
    365 +                        field="name",
    366 +                    )
    367 +                )
    368 +            elif expected_name and name != expected_name:
    369 +                errors.append(
    370 +                    issue(
    371 +                        "NAME_PATH_MISMATCH",
    372 +                        f"name {name!r} does not match basename {expected_name!r}",
    373 +                        line_number=line_number,
    374 +                        relative_path=relative_path or None,
    375 +                        field="name",
    376 +                    )
    377 +                )
    378 +
    379 +            expected_parent = str(PurePosixPath(relative_path).parent) if relative_path else
         ""
    380 +            if expected_parent == ".":
    381 +                expected_parent = ""
    382 +            if relative_path and parent_relative_path != expected_parent:
    383 +                errors.append(
    384 +                    issue(
    385 +                        "PARENT_PATH_MISMATCH",
    386 +                        f"parent_relative_path {parent_relative_path!r} does not match derive
         d parent {expected_parent!r}",
    387 +                        line_number=line_number,
    388 +                        relative_path=relative_path,
    389 +                        field="parent_relative_path",
    390 +                    )
    391 +                )
    392 +
    393 +            if parent_directory_id and not DIRECTORY_ID_PATTERN.fullmatch(parent_directory_id
         ):
    394 +                errors.append(
    395 +                    issue(
    396 +                        "INVALID_PARENT_DIRECTORY_ID",
    397 +                        "parent_directory_id must be empty or match ^2\\d{19}$",
    398 +                        line_number=line_number,
    399 +                        relative_path=relative_path or None,
    400 +                        field="parent_directory_id",
    401 +                    )
    402 +                )
    403 +
    404 +            if file_id and not FILE_ID_PATTERN.fullmatch(file_id):
    405 +                errors.append(
    406 +                    issue(
    407 +                        "INVALID_FILE_ID",
    408 +                        "file_id must be empty or match ^1\\d{19}$",
    409 +                        line_number=line_number,
    410 +                        relative_path=relative_path or None,
    411 +                        field="file_id",
    412 +                    )
    413 +                )
    414 +
    415 +            if directory_id and not DIRECTORY_ID_PATTERN.fullmatch(directory_id):
    416 +                errors.append(
    417 +                    issue(
    418 +                        "INVALID_DIRECTORY_ID",
    419 +                        "directory_id must be empty or match ^2\\d{19}$",
    420 +                        line_number=line_number,
    421 +                        relative_path=relative_path or None,
    422 +                        field="directory_id",
    423 +                    )
    424 +                )
    425 +
    426 +            if row["id_source"] not in VALID_ID_SOURCES:
    427 +                errors.append(
    428 +                    issue(
    429 +                        "INVALID_ID_SOURCE",
    430 +                        f"id_source must be one of {sorted(VALID_ID_SOURCES)}, got {row['id_s
         ource']!r}",
    431 +                        line_number=line_number,
    432 +                        relative_path=relative_path or None,
    433 +                        field="id_source",
    434 +                    )
    435 +                )
    436 +
    437 +            has_file_id = bool(file_id)
    438 +            has_directory_id = bool(directory_id)
    439 +            if has_file_id and has_directory_id:
    440 +                errors.append(
    441 +                    issue(
    442 +                        "AMBIGUOUS_ROW_ID",
    443 +                        "row may not contain both file_id and directory_id",
    444 +                        line_number=line_number,
    445 +                        relative_path=relative_path or None,
    446 +                    )
    447 +                )
    448 +
    449 +            expected_extension = PurePosixPath(name).suffix if name else ""
    450 +            if object_type == "file":
    451 +                if has_directory_id:
    452 +                    errors.append(
    453 +                        issue(
    454 +                            "FILE_ROW_HAS_DIRECTORY_ID",
    455 +                            "file rows must leave directory_id empty",
    456 +                            line_number=line_number,
    457 +                            relative_path=relative_path or None,
    458 +                        )
    459 +                    )
    460 +                if not is_excluded and not has_file_id:
    461 +                    errors.append(
    462 +                        issue(
    463 +                            "NON_EXCLUDED_FILE_MISSING_ID",
    464 +                            "non-excluded file row must have a file_id",
    465 +                            line_number=line_number,
    466 +                            relative_path=relative_path or None,
    467 +                        )
    468 +                    )
    469 +                if row["extension"] != expected_extension:
    470 +                    errors.append(
    471 +                        issue(
    472 +                            "EXTENSION_MISMATCH",
    473 +                            f"extension {row['extension']!r} does not match derived extension
          {expected_extension!r}",
    474 +                            line_number=line_number,
    475 +                            relative_path=relative_path or None,
    476 +                            field="extension",
    477 +                        )
    478 +                    )
    479 +            elif object_type == "directory":
    480 +                if has_file_id:
    481 +                    errors.append(
    482 +                        issue(
    483 +                            "DIRECTORY_ROW_HAS_FILE_ID",
    484 +                            "directory rows must leave file_id empty",
    485 +                            line_number=line_number,
    486 +                            relative_path=relative_path or None,
    487 +                        )
    488 +                    )
    489 +                if not is_excluded and not has_directory_id:
    490 +                    errors.append(
    491 +                        issue(
    492 +                            "NON_EXCLUDED_DIRECTORY_MISSING_ID",
    493 +                            "non-excluded directory row must have a directory_id",
    494 +                            line_number=line_number,
    495 +                            relative_path=relative_path or None,
    496 +                        )
    497 +                    )
    498 +                if row["extension"]:
    499 +                    errors.append(
    500 +                        issue(
    501 +                            "DIRECTORY_EXTENSION_NOT_EMPTY",
    502 +                            "directory rows must leave extension empty",
    503 +                            line_number=line_number,
    504 +                            relative_path=relative_path or None,
    505 +                            field="extension",
    506 +                        )
    507 +                    )
    508 +
    509 +            if not is_excluded and not (has_file_id ^ has_directory_id):
    510 +                errors.append(
    511 +                    issue(
    512 +                        "NON_EXCLUDED_ROW_ID_CARDINALITY",
    513 +                        "non-excluded rows must have exactly one non-empty ID field",
    514 +                        line_number=line_number,
    515 +                        relative_path=relative_path or None,
    516 +                    )
    517 +                )
    518 +
    519 +            if is_excluded and not (has_file_id or has_directory_id):
    520 +                warnings.append(
    521 +                    issue(
    522 +                        "EXCLUDED_ROW_WITHOUT_ID",
    523 +                        "excluded row carries no physical ID",
    524 +                        line_number=line_number,
    525 +                        relative_path=relative_path or None,
    526 +                    )
    527 +                )
    528 +
    529 +            typed_rows.append(
    530 +                {
    531 +                    **row,
    532 +                    "line_number": line_number,
    533 +                    "is_excluded": is_excluded,
    534 +                    "exists_on_disk": exists_on_disk,
    535 +                }
    536 +            )
    537 +
    538 +    return typed_rows, errors, warnings
    539 +
    540 +
    541 +def validate_registry_integrity(rows: list[dict[str, Any]], repo_root: Path) -> list[dict[str
         , Any]]:
    542 +    errors: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
    543 +    rows_by_path: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
    544 +    directory_rows_by_path: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
    545 +    file_ids: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
    546 +    directory_ids: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
    547 +
    548 +    for row in rows:
    549 +        relative_path = str(row["relative_path"])
    550 +        key = path_key(relative_path)
    551 +        existing_path_row = rows_by_path.get(key)
    552 +        if existing_path_row is not None:
    553 +            errors.append(
    554 +                issue(
    555 +                    "DUPLICATE_RELATIVE_PATH",
    556 +                    f"relative_path duplicates line {existing_path_row['line_number']}",
    557 +                    line_number=row["line_number"],
    558 +                    relative_path=relative_path,
    559 +                )
    560 +            )
    561 +        else:
    562 +            rows_by_path[key] = row
    563 +
    564 +        if row["object_type"] == "directory":
    565 +            directory_rows_by_path[key] = row
    566 +
    567 +        file_id = str(row["file_id"])
    568 +        if file_id:
    569 +            existing = file_ids.get(file_id)
    570 +            if existing is not None:
    571 +                errors.append(
    572 +                    issue(
    573 +                        "DUPLICATE_FILE_ID",
    574 +                        f"file_id duplicates line {existing['line_number']}",
    575 +                        line_number=row["line_number"],
    576 +                        relative_path=relative_path,
    577 +                        field="file_id",
    578 +                    )
    579 +                )
    580 +            else:
    581 +                file_ids[file_id] = row
    582 +
    583 +        directory_id = str(row["directory_id"])
    584 +        if directory_id:
    585 +            existing = directory_ids.get(directory_id)
    586 +            if existing is not None:
    587 +                errors.append(
    588 +                    issue(
    589 +                        "DUPLICATE_DIRECTORY_ID",
    590 +                        f"directory_id duplicates line {existing['line_number']}",
    591 +                        line_number=row["line_number"],
    592 +                        relative_path=relative_path,
    593 +                        field="directory_id",
    594 +                    )
    595 +                )
    596 +            else:
    597 +                directory_ids[directory_id] = row
    598 +
    599 +        path_on_disk = repo_root.joinpath(*relative_path.split("/"))
    600 +        exists_on_disk = bool(row["exists_on_disk"])
    601 +        if exists_on_disk:
    602 +            if row["object_type"] == "file" and not path_on_disk.is_file():
    603 +                errors.append(
    604 +                    issue(
    605 +                        "FILE_MISSING_ON_DISK",
    606 +                        "row declares exists_on_disk=True but file is missing",
    607 +                        line_number=row["line_number"],
    608 +                        relative_path=relative_path,
    609 +                    )
    610 +                )
    611 +            if row["object_type"] == "directory" and not path_on_disk.is_dir():
    612 +                errors.append(
    613 +                    issue(
    614 +                        "DIRECTORY_MISSING_ON_DISK",
    615 +                        "row declares exists_on_disk=True but directory is missing",
    616 +                        line_number=row["line_number"],
    617 +                        relative_path=relative_path,
    618 +                    )
    619 +                )
    620 +        elif path_on_disk.exists():
    621 +            errors.append(
    622 +                issue(
    623 +                    "EXISTS_ON_DISK_MISMATCH",
    624 +                    "row declares exists_on_disk=False but path exists",
    625 +                    line_number=row["line_number"],
    626 +                    relative_path=relative_path,
    627 +                )
    628 +            )
    629 +
    630 +    for row in rows:
    631 +        relative_path = str(row["relative_path"])
    632 +        parent_relative_path = str(row["parent_relative_path"])
    633 +        parent_directory_id = str(row["parent_directory_id"])
    634 +        if not parent_relative_path:
    635 +            if parent_directory_id:
    636 +                errors.append(
    637 +                    issue(
    638 +                        "ROOT_ROW_HAS_PARENT_ID",
    639 +                        "root-level rows must leave parent_directory_id empty",
    640 +                        line_number=row["line_number"],
    641 +                        relative_path=relative_path,
    642 +                        field="parent_directory_id",
    643 +                    )
    644 +                )
    645 +            continue
    646 +
    647 +        parent_row = directory_rows_by_path.get(path_key(parent_relative_path))
    648 +        if parent_row is None:
    649 +            errors.append(
    650 +                issue(
    651 +                    "MISSING_PARENT_ROW",
    652 +                    "parent_relative_path does not resolve to a directory row",
    653 +                    line_number=row["line_number"],
    654 +                    relative_path=relative_path,
    655 +                    field="parent_relative_path",
    656 +                )
    657 +            )
    658 +            continue
    659 +
    660 +        expected_parent_id = str(parent_row["directory_id"])
    661 +        if not expected_parent_id:
    662 +            errors.append(
    663 +                issue(
    664 +                    "PARENT_ROW_MISSING_DIRECTORY_ID",
    665 +                    "parent directory row has no directory_id",
    666 +                    line_number=row["line_number"],
    667 +                    relative_path=relative_path,
    668 +                    field="parent_directory_id",
    669 +                )
    670 +            )
    671 +        elif parent_directory_id != expected_parent_id:
    672 +            errors.append(
    673 +                issue(
    674 +                    "PARENT_DIRECTORY_ID_MISMATCH",
    675 +                    f"parent_directory_id {parent_directory_id!r} does not match parent row d
         irectory_id {expected_parent_id!r}",
    676 +                    line_number=row["line_number"],
    677 +                    relative_path=relative_path,
    678 +                    field="parent_directory_id",
    679 +                )
    680 +            )
    681 +
    682 +    return errors
    683 +
    684 +
    685 +def validate_anchors_and_directories(
    686 +    *,
    687 +    repo_root: Path,
    688 +    config: dict[str, Any],
    689 +    classification_rules: dict[str, Any],
    690 +    dir_schema: dict[str, Any] | None,
    691 +    registry_rows: list[dict[str, Any]],
    692 +) -> tuple[list[dict[str, Any]], dict[str, int]]:
    693 +    errors: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
    694 +    anchor_name = str(config["directory_identity_mechanism"]["anchor_filename"])
    695 +    governed_dirs = discover_governed_directories(repo_root, config, classification_rules)
    696 +
    697 +    registry_directory_rows = {
    698 +        path_key(str(row["relative_path"])): row
    699 +        for row in registry_rows
    700 +        if row["object_type"] == "directory"
    701 +    }
    702 +    anchors_seen: dict[str, Path] = {}
    703 +    anchor_count = 0
    704 +
    705 +    for anchor_path in repo_root.rglob(anchor_name):
    706 +        if not anchor_path.is_file():
    707 +            continue
    708 +        anchor_count += 1
    709 +        relative_dir = normalize_absolute_path(anchor_path.parent, repo_root)
    710 +        relative_dir_key = path_key(relative_dir)
    711 +
    712 +        previous_anchor = anchors_seen.get(relative_dir_key)
    713 +        if previous_anchor is not None:
    714 +            errors.append(
    715 +                issue(
    716 +                    "MULTIPLE_ANCHORS_FOR_DIRECTORY",
    717 +                    f"directory already had anchor at {previous_anchor}",
    718 +                    relative_path=relative_dir or None,
    719 +                )
    720 +            )
    721 +            continue
    722 +        anchors_seen[relative_dir_key] = anchor_path
    723 +
    724 +        try:
    725 +            payload = load_json(anchor_path)
    726 +        except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
    727 +            errors.append(
    728 +                issue(
    729 +                    "INVALID_ANCHOR_JSON",
    730 +                    f"anchor is not valid JSON: {exc}",
    731 +                    relative_path=relative_dir or None,
    732 +                )
    733 +            )
    734 +            continue
    735 +
    736 +        anchor_errors = validate_dir_anchor_payload(
    737 +            payload,
    738 +            expected_relative_path=relative_dir,
    739 +            schema=dir_schema,
    740 +        )
    741 +        for message in anchor_errors:
    742 +            errors.append(
    743 +                issue(
    744 +                    "INVALID_DIR_ANCHOR",
    745 +                    message,
    746 +                    relative_path=relative_dir or None,
    747 +                )
    748 +            )
    749 +
    750 +        registry_row = registry_directory_rows.get(relative_dir_key)
    751 +        if registry_row is None:
    752 +            errors.append(
    753 +                issue(
    754 +                    "ORPHAN_DIR_ANCHOR",
    755 +                    "anchor exists on disk but no directory row exists in physical_id_registr
         y.csv",
    756 +                    relative_path=relative_dir or None,
    757 +                )
    758 +            )
    759 +            continue
    760 +
    761 +        payload_dir_id = payload.get("dir_id") if isinstance(payload, dict) else None
    762 +        registry_dir_id = str(registry_row["directory_id"])
    763 +        if payload_dir_id != registry_dir_id:
    764 +            errors.append(
    765 +                issue(
    766 +                    "ANCHOR_DIRECTORY_ID_MISMATCH",
    767 +                    f"anchor dir_id {payload_dir_id!r} does not match registry directory_id {
         registry_dir_id!r}",
    768 +                    line_number=registry_row["line_number"],
    769 +                    relative_path=relative_dir or None,
    770 +                )
    771 +            )
    772 +
    773 +    for relative_dir in sorted(governed_dirs, key=str.casefold):
    774 +        directory_path = repo_root.joinpath(*relative_dir.split("/"))
    775 +        anchor_path = directory_path / anchor_name
    776 +        if not anchor_path.is_file():
    777 +            errors.append(
    778 +                issue(
    779 +                    "MISSING_DIR_ANCHOR",
    780 +                    "governed directory is missing .dir_id anchor",
    781 +                    relative_path=relative_dir,
    782 +                )
    783 +            )
    784 +
    785 +        registry_row = registry_directory_rows.get(path_key(relative_dir))
    786 +        if registry_row is None:
    787 +            errors.append(
    788 +                issue(
    789 +                    "MISSING_DIRECTORY_REGISTRY_ROW",
    790 +                    "governed directory is missing from physical_id_registry.csv",
    791 +                    relative_path=relative_dir,
    792 +                )
    793 +            )
    794 +        elif registry_row["is_excluded"]:
    795 +            errors.append(
    796 +                issue(
    797 +                    "GOVERNED_DIRECTORY_MARKED_EXCLUDED",
    798 +                    "governed directory row is unexpectedly marked excluded",
    799 +                    line_number=registry_row["line_number"],
    800 +                    relative_path=relative_dir,
    801 +                )
    802 +            )
    803 +
    804 +    for registry_row in registry_directory_rows.values():
    805 +        relative_dir = str(registry_row["relative_path"])
    806 +        if not registry_row["is_excluded"] and registry_row["exists_on_disk"] and relative_di
         r not in governed_dirs:
    807 +            errors.append(
    808 +                issue(
    809 +                    "REGISTRY_DIRECTORY_NOT_GOVERNED",
    810 +                    "directory row exists on disk but was not discovered as a governed direct
         ory",
    811 +                    line_number=registry_row["line_number"],
    812 +                    relative_path=relative_dir,
    813 +                )
    814 +            )
    815 +
    816 +    return errors, {
    817 +        "governed_directories_on_disk": len(governed_dirs),
    818 +        "anchors_on_disk": anchor_count,
    819 +    }
    820 +
    821 +
    822 +def build_report(
    823 +    *,
    824 +    errors: list[dict[str, Any]],
    825 +    warnings: list[dict[str, Any]],
    826 +    registry_rows: list[dict[str, Any]],
    827 +    directory_metrics: dict[str, int],
    828 +    config_path: Path,
    829 +    registry_path: Path,
    830 +    report_path: Path,
    831 +) -> dict[str, Any]:
    832 +    non_excluded_rows = sum(1 for row in registry_rows if not row["is_excluded"])
    833 +    file_rows = sum(1 for row in registry_rows if row["object_type"] == "file")
    834 +    directory_rows = sum(1 for row in registry_rows if row["object_type"] == "directory")
    835 +    physical_status = "PASS" if not errors else "FAIL"
    836 +
    837 +    return {
    838 +        "gate": "G-02",
    839 +        "validated_at_utc": utc_now(),
    840 +        "physical_status": physical_status,
    841 +        "inputs": {
    842 +            "config": str(config_path.relative_to(REPO_ROOT)).replace("\\", "/"),
    843 +            "registry": str(registry_path.relative_to(REPO_ROOT)).replace("\\", "/"),
    844 +        },
    845 +        "output": str(report_path.relative_to(REPO_ROOT)).replace("\\", "/"),
    846 +        "summary": {
    847 +            "registry_rows": len(registry_rows),
    848 +            "registry_file_rows": file_rows,
    849 +            "registry_directory_rows": directory_rows,
    850 +            "non_excluded_rows": non_excluded_rows,
    851 +            "excluded_rows": len(registry_rows) - non_excluded_rows,
    852 +            **directory_metrics,
    853 +            "error_count": len(errors),
    854 +            "warning_count": len(warnings),
    855 +        },
    856 +        "checks": {
    857 +            "registry_has_exact_11_columns": not any(error["code"] == "INVALID_HEADER" for er
         ror in errors),
    858 +            "non_excluded_rows_have_physical_ids": not any(
    859 +                error["code"]
    860 +                in {
    861 +                    "NON_EXCLUDED_FILE_MISSING_ID",
    862 +                    "NON_EXCLUDED_DIRECTORY_MISSING_ID",
    863 +                    "NON_EXCLUDED_ROW_ID_CARDINALITY",
    864 +                }
    865 +                for error in errors
    866 +            ),
    867 +            "parent_linkage_valid": not any(
    868 +                error["code"]
    869 +                in {
    870 +                    "MISSING_PARENT_ROW",
    871 +                    "PARENT_ROW_MISSING_DIRECTORY_ID",
    872 +                    "PARENT_DIRECTORY_ID_MISMATCH",
    873 +                    "ROOT_ROW_HAS_PARENT_ID",
    874 +                }
    875 +                for error in errors
    876 +            ),
    877 +            "no_duplicate_ids": not any(
    878 +                error["code"] in {"DUPLICATE_FILE_ID", "DUPLICATE_DIRECTORY_ID"} for error in
          errors
    879 +            ),
    880 +            "no_orphan_dir_anchors": not any(
    881 +                error["code"] in {"ORPHAN_DIR_ANCHOR", "MISSING_DIR_ANCHOR"} for error in err
         ors
    882 +            ),
    883 +            "registry_paths_match_filesystem": not any(
    884 +                error["code"]
    885 +                in {
    886 +                    "FILE_MISSING_ON_DISK",
    887 +                    "DIRECTORY_MISSING_ON_DISK",
    888 +                    "EXISTS_ON_DISK_MISMATCH",
    889 +                    "REGISTRY_DIRECTORY_NOT_GOVERNED",
    890 +                }
    891 +                for error in errors
    892 +            ),
    893 +        },
    894 +        "errors": errors,
    895 +        "warnings": warnings,
    896 +    }
    897 +
    898 +
    899 +def parse_args(argv: list[str]) -> argparse.Namespace:
    900 +    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="PH-03 physical identity validator")
    901 +    parser.add_argument("--config", default=str(DEFAULT_CONFIG_PATH), help="Path to physical_
         id_config.json")
    902 +    return parser.parse_args(argv)
    903 +
    904 +
    905 +def main(argv: list[str]) -> int:
    906 +    args = parse_args(argv)
    907 +    config_path = Path(args.config)
    908 +    if not config_path.is_absolute():
    909 +        config_path = (REPO_ROOT / config_path).resolve()
    910 +
    911 +    if not config_path.is_file():
    912 +        print(f"ERROR: config not found: {config_path}", file=sys.stderr)
    913 +        return 2
    914 +    if not DEFAULT_REGISTRY_PATH.is_file():
    915 +        print(f"ERROR: registry not found: {DEFAULT_REGISTRY_PATH}", file=sys.stderr)
    916 +        return 2
    917 +    if not DEFAULT_DIR_SCHEMA_PATH.is_file():
    918 +        print(f"ERROR: dir_id schema not found: {DEFAULT_DIR_SCHEMA_PATH}", file=sys.stderr)
    919 +        return 2
    920 +    if not DEFAULT_CLASSIFICATION_RULES_PATH.is_file():
    921 +        print(f"ERROR: classification rules not found: {DEFAULT_CLASSIFICATION_RULES_PATH}",
         file=sys.stderr)
    922 +        return 2
    923 +
    924 +    try:
    925 +        config = load_json(config_path)
    926 +        if not isinstance(config, dict):
    927 +            raise ValueError("config root must be a JSON object")
    928 +        dir_schema = load_json(DEFAULT_DIR_SCHEMA_PATH)
    929 +        classification_rules = load_classification_rules(DEFAULT_CLASSIFICATION_RULES_PATH)
    930 +        registry_rows, registry_errors, registry_warnings = load_registry_rows(DEFAULT_REGIST
         RY_PATH)
    931 +        integrity_errors = validate_registry_integrity(registry_rows, REPO_ROOT)
    932 +        anchor_errors, directory_metrics = validate_anchors_and_directories(
    933 +            repo_root=REPO_ROOT,
    934 +            config=config,
    935 +            classification_rules=classification_rules,

     59 +def normalize_relative_path(path_value: str) -> str:
     60 +    value = str(path_value).replace("\\", "/")
     61 +    while value.startswith("./"):
     62 +        value = value[2:]
     63 +    value = re.sub(r"/+", "/", value)
     64 +    value = value.rstrip("/")
     65 +    if value in {"", "."}:
     66 +        return ""
     67 +
     68 +    parts: list[str] = []
     69 +    for segment in value.split("/"):
     70 +        if segment in {"", "."}:
     71 +            continue
     72 +        if segment == "..":
     73 +            if parts:
     74 +                parts.pop()
     75 +            continue
     76 +        parts.append(segment)
     77 +    return "/".join(parts)
     78 +
     79 +
     80 +def normalize_absolute_path(path: Path, repo_root: Path) -> str:
     81 +    return normalize_relative_path(os.path.relpath(path, repo_root))
     82 +
     83 +
     84 +def path_key(path_value: str) -> str:
     85 +    normalized = normalize_relative_path(path_value)
     86 +    return normalized.casefold() if os.name == "nt" else normalized
     87 +

     89 +def parse_bool(value: str, *, field: str, line_number: int, errors: list[dict[str, Any]]) ->
         bool:
     90 +    if value == "True":
     91 +        return True
     92 +    if value == "False":
     93 +        return False
     94 +    errors.append(
     95 +        issue(
     96 +            "INVALID_BOOLEAN",
     97 +            f"{field} must be True or False, got {value!r}",
     98 +            line_number=line_number,
     99 +            field=field,
    100 +        )
    101 +    )
    102 +    return False
    103 +
    104 +
    105 +def parse_datetime(value: Any) -> bool:
    106 +    if not isinstance(value, str):
    107 +        return False
    108 +    candidate = value.replace("Z", "+00:00")
    109 +    try:
    110 +        datetime.fromisoformat(candidate)
    111 +    except ValueError:
    112 +        return False
    113 +    return True

    141 +def classify_path(rel_path: str, object_type: str, rules_data: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, A
         ny]:
    142 +    default_class = rules_data.get("default_scope_class", "module_owned")
    143 +    classifications = rules_data.get("classifications", {})
    144 +    rules = rules_data.get("rules", [])
    145 +
    146 +    scope_class = default_class
    147 +    match_path = rel_path.replace("\\", "/")
    148 +    match_path_for_rules = f"{match_path}/" if object_type == "directory" and not match_path.
         endswith("/") else match_path
    149 +
    150 +    for rule in rules:
    151 +        match_type = rule.get("match_type")
    152 +        values = rule.get("values", [])
    153 +        matched = False
    154 +        if match_type == "path_prefix":
    155 +            matched = any(match_path_for_rules.startswith(value) or match_path.startswith(val
         ue) for value in values)
    156 +        elif match_type == "path_contains":
    157 +            matched = any(value in match_path_for_rules or value in match_path for value in v
         alues)
    158 +        if matched:
    159 +            scope_class = str(rule.get("scope_class", scope_class))
    160 +            break
    161 +
    162 +    return classifications.get(scope_class, {"object_scope_class": scope_class}) | {"object_s
         cope_class": scope_class}
