    189 +def validate_dir_anchor_payload(
    190 +    payload: Any,
    191 +    *,
    192 +    expected_relative_path: str,
    193 +    schema: dict[str, Any] | None,
    194 +) -> list[str]:
    195 +    errors: list[str] = []
    196 +
    197 +    if schema is not None:
    198 +        try:
    199 +            from jsonschema import Draft202012Validator
    200 +        except ImportError:
    201 +            schema = None
    202 +        else:
    203 +            validator = Draft202012Validator(schema)
    204 +            errors.extend(error.message for error in validator.iter_errors(payload))
    205 +
    206 +    if not isinstance(payload, dict):
    207 +        return errors + ["anchor payload must be a JSON object"]
    208 +
    209 +    required_keys = {
    210 +        "dir_id",
    211 +        "allocated_at_utc",
    212 +        "allocator_version",
    213 +        "project_root_id",
    214 +        "relative_path",
    215 +    }
    216 +    if set(payload) != required_keys:
    217 +        missing = sorted(required_keys - set(payload))
    218 +        extra = sorted(set(payload) - required_keys)
    219 +        if missing:
    220 +            errors.append(f"missing keys: {', '.join(missing)}")
    221 +        if extra:
    222 +            errors.append(f"unexpected keys: {', '.join(extra)}")
    223 +
    224 +    dir_id = payload.get("dir_id")
    225 +    if not isinstance(dir_id, str) or not DIRECTORY_ID_PATTERN.fullmatch(dir_id):
    226 +        errors.append("dir_id must match ^2\\d{19}$")
    227 +
    228 +    allocated_at = payload.get("allocated_at_utc")
    229 +    if not parse_datetime(allocated_at):
    230 +        errors.append("allocated_at_utc must be an ISO-8601 datetime")
    231 +
    232 +    allocator_version = payload.get("allocator_version")
    233 +    if not isinstance(allocator_version, str) or not allocator_version.strip():
    234 +        errors.append("allocator_version must be a non-empty string")
    235 +
    236 +    project_root_id = payload.get("project_root_id")
    237 +    if project_root_id is not None and (
    238 +        not isinstance(project_root_id, str) or not DIRECTORY_ID_PATTERN.fullmatch(project_ro
         ot_id)
    239 +    ):
    240 +        errors.append("project_root_id must be null or match ^2\\d{19}$")
    241 +
    242 +    relative_path = payload.get("relative_path")
    243 +    if not isinstance(relative_path, str) or not relative_path:
    244 +        errors.append("relative_path must be a non-empty string")
    245 +    else:
    246 +        normalized = normalize_relative_path(relative_path)
    247 +        if normalized != relative_path:
    248 +            errors.append("relative_path must already be normalized")
    249 +        if not PATH_PATTERN.fullmatch(relative_path):
    250 +            errors.append("relative_path does not satisfy the path normalization contract")
    251 +        if relative_path != expected_relative_path:
    252 +            errors.append(
    253 +                f"relative_path {relative_path!r} does not match anchor location {expected_re
         lative_path!r}"
    254 +            )
    255 +
    256 +    return errors

    474 +                            line_number=line_number,
    475 +                            relative_path=relative_path or None,
    476 +                            field="extension",
    477 +                        )
    478 +                    )
    479 +            elif object_type == "directory":
    480 +                if has_file_id:
    481 +                    errors.append(
    482 +                        issue(
    483 +                            "DIRECTORY_ROW_HAS_FILE_ID",
    484 +                            "directory rows must leave file_id empty",
    485 +                            line_number=line_number,
    486 +                            relative_path=relative_path or None,
    487 +                        )
    488 +                    )
    489 +                if not is_excluded and not has_directory_id:
    490 +                    errors.append(
    491 +                        issue(
    492 +                            "NON_EXCLUDED_DIRECTORY_MISSING_ID",
    493 +                            "non-excluded directory row must have a directory_id",
    494 +                            line_number=line_number,
    495 +                            relative_path=relative_path or None,
    496 +                        )
    497 +                    )
    498 +                if row["extension"]:

    500 +                        issue(

    502 +                            "directory rows must leave extension empty",
    503 +                            line_number=line_number,
    504 +                            relative_path=relative_path or None,
    505 +                            field="extension",
    506 +                        )
    507 +                    )
    508 +
    509 +            if not is_excluded and not (has_file_id ^ has_directory_id):
    510 +                errors.append(
    511 +                    issue(
    512 +                        "NON_EXCLUDED_ROW_ID_CARDINALITY",
    513 +                        "non-excluded rows must have exactly one non-empty ID field",
    514 +                        line_number=line_number,
    515 +                        relative_path=relative_path or None,
    516 +                    )
    517 +                )
    518 +
    519 +            if is_excluded and not (has_file_id or has_directory_id):
    520 +                warnings.append(
    521 +                    issue(
    522 +                        "EXCLUDED_ROW_WITHOUT_ID",
    523 +                        "excluded row carries no physical ID",
    524 +                        line_number=line_number,
    525 +                        relative_path=relative_path or None,
    526 +                    )
    527 +                )
    528 +
    529 +            typed_rows.append(
    530 +                {
    531 +                    **row,
    532 +                    "line_number": line_number,
    533 +                    "is_excluded": is_excluded,
    534 +                    "exists_on_disk": exists_on_disk,
    535 +                }
    536 +            )
    537 +
    538 +    return typed_rows, errors, warnings

    306 +def classify_scope(relative_path: str, object_type: str, rules_data: dict[str, object]) -> st
         r:
    307 +    default_class = str(rules_data.get("default_scope_class", "module_owned"))
    308 +    scope_class = default_class
    309 +    match_path = relative_path.replace("\\", "/")
    310 +    match_path_for_rules = f"{match_path}/" if object_type == "directory" and not match_path.
         endswith("/") else match_path

    312 +    for rule in rules_data.get("rules", []):
    313 +        if not isinstance(rule, dict):
    314 +            continue
    315 +        values = [str(value) for value in rule.get("values", [])]
    316 +        matched = False
    317 +        if rule.get("match_type") == "path_prefix":
    318 +            matched = any(match_path_for_rules.startswith(value) or match_path.startswith(val
         ue) for value in values)
    319 +        elif rule.get("match_type") == "path_contains":
    320 +            matched = any(value in match_path_for_rules or value in match_path for value in v
         alues)
    321 +        if matched:
    322 +            scope_class = str(rule.get("scope_class", scope_class))
    323 +            break
    324 +
    325 +    return scope_class

    140 +        print("\n1. CHECKING ARTIFACT EXISTENCE")

    143 +            ("file registry", self.file_registry_path, True),
    144 +            ("module catalog", self.module_catalog_path, True),
    145 +            ("process step catalog", self.process_step_catalog_path, True),
    146 +            ("module schema", self.module_schema_path, True),
    147 +            ("identifier map", self.identifier_map_path, True),

    149 +            ("physical validation report", self.physical_report_path, False),
    150 +        ]
    151 +
    152 +        for label, path, required in required_paths:
    153 +            if path.exists():
    154 +                print(f"✓ {label}: {path.name}")
    155 +                self.info.append(f"{label.title()} present: {path.name}")
    156 +                continue
    157 +            message = f"Missing {label}: {path}"
    158 +            if required:
    159 +                print(f"✗ {message}")
    160 +                self.alignment_errors.append(message)

    162 +                print(f"⚠ {message}")

    165 +    def _load_csv_rows(self, path: Path, label: str) -> tuple[list[dict[str, str]], list[str]
         ]:
    166 +        if not path.exists():
    167 +            return [], []
    168 +
    169 +        try:
    170 +            content = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig")
    171 +            reader = csv.DictReader(StringIO(content))
    172 +            rows = [
    173 +                row
    174 +                for row in reader
    175 +                if row and any((value or "").strip() for value in row.values())
    176 +            ]
    177 +            return rows, reader.fieldnames or []
    178 +        except Exception as exc:
    179 +            self.alignment_errors.append(f"Error loading {label}: {exc}")
    180 +            return [], []
    181 +
    182 +    def _load_json(self, path: Path, label: str, *, required: bool = True) -> dict[str, Any]:
    183 +        if not path.exists():
    184 +            if required:
    185 +                self.alignment_errors.append(f"Missing {label}: {path}")
    186 +            return {}
    187 +
    188 +        try:
    189 +            with path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as handle:
    190 +                payload = json.load(handle)
    191 +        except Exception as exc:
    192 +            self.alignment_errors.append(f"Error loading {label}: {exc}")
    193 +            return {}
    194 +
    195 +        if not isinstance(payload, dict):
    196 +            self.alignment_errors.append(f"{label.title()} is not a JSON object: {path}")
    197 +            return {}
    198 +        return payload
    199 +
    200 +    def _load_process_yaml(self) -> tuple[Path | None, dict[str, Any]]:
    201 +        for candidate in self.process_source_candidates:
    202 +            if not candidate.exists():
    203 +                continue
    204 +            try:
    205 +                with candidate.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as handle:
    206 +                    payload = yaml.safe_load(handle)
    207 +            except Exception as exc:
    208 +                self.alignment_errors.append(f"Error loading process YAML {candidate}: {exc}"
         )
    209 +                return candidate, {}
    210 +            if isinstance(payload, dict):
    211 +                return candidate, payload
    212 +            self.alignment_errors.append(f"Process YAML is not a mapping: {candidate}")
    213 +            return candidate, {}
    214 +        self.alignment_errors.append("No process YAML source was found for comparison.")
    215 +        return None, {}
    216 +
    217 +    def _normalize_path(self, path_text: str) -> str:
    218 +        raw = (path_text or "").strip().replace("\\", "/")
    219 +        return PurePosixPath(raw.lstrip("./")).as_posix() if raw else ""
    220 +
    221 +    def _parse_utc(self, value: str) -> bool:
    222 +        if not value or not UTC_PATTERN.search(value):
    223 +            return False
    224 +        try:
    225 +            datetime.fromisoformat(value.replace("Z", "+00:00"))
    226 +        except ValueError:
    227 +            return False
    228 +        return True

    259 +    def _validate_module_catalog_schema(self, module_catalog: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
    260 +        print("\n3. VALIDATING MODULE CATALOG SCHEMA")
    261 +        print("-" * 80)

    277 +            path = ".".join(str(part) for part in error.path) or "<root>"

         message}")
    279 +        if not errors:
    280 +            self.info.append("Module catalog passes schema validation.")

    282 +    def _validate_module_catalog(self, module_catalog: dict[str, Any], identifier_map: dict[s
         tr, Any]) -> None:
    283 +        modules = module_catalog.get("modules", [])
    284 +        if not isinstance(modules, list):
    285 +            self.alignment_errors.append("module_catalog.json must contain a modules array")
    286 +            return
    287 +
    288 +        seen_module_ids: set[str] = set()
    289 +        seen_symbols: set[str] = set()
    290 +        alias_symbols = set((identifier_map.get("aliases") or {}).keys())
    291 +
    292 +        for module in modules:
    293 +            module_id = str(module.get("module_id", ""))
    294 +            canonical_symbol = str(module.get("canonical_symbol", ""))
    295 +            module_name = str(module.get("module_name", ""))
    296 +            if not MODULE_ID_PATTERN.fullmatch(module_id):
    297 +                self.alignment_errors.append(f"Invalid module_catalog.module_id: {module_id!r
         }")
    298 +            if module_id in seen_module_ids:
    299 +                self.alignment_errors.append(f"Duplicate module_catalog.module_id: {module_id
         }")
    300 +            seen_module_ids.add(module_id)
    301 +
    302 +            if not canonical_symbol:
    303 +                self.alignment_errors.append("module_catalog canonical_symbol may not be blan
         k")
    304 +            if canonical_symbol in seen_symbols:
    305 +                self.alignment_errors.append(f"Duplicate module_catalog canonical_symbol: {ca
         nonical_symbol}")
    306 +            seen_symbols.add(canonical_symbol)
    307 +
    308 +            if canonical_symbol in alias_symbols:
    309 +                self.alignment_errors.append(
    310 +                    f"Alias symbol {canonical_symbol} must not appear as a module_catalog row
         "
    311 +                )
    312 +            if not module_name:
    313 +                self.alignment_errors.append(f"module_catalog row {canonical_symbol!r} has bl
         ank module_name")
    314 +
    315 +        self.info.append(f"Module catalog rows checked: {len(modules)}")

    317 +    def _validate_process_catalog(

    331 +        }
    332 +        id_steps = identifier_map.get("process_steps", {})
    333 +        id_steps_by_number = {
    334 +            int(step_payload["step_number"]): step_payload
    335 +            for step_payload in id_steps.values()
    336 +            if isinstance(step_payload, dict) and step_payload.get("step_number") is not None
    337 +        }
    338 +        seen_step_ids: set[str] = set()
    339 +
    340 +        for step in steps:
    341 +            step_number = int(step.get("step_number", 0))
    342 +            process_step_id = str(step.get("process_step_id", ""))
    343 +            module_id = str(step.get("module_id", ""))
    344 +            module_symbol = str(step.get("module_symbol", ""))
    345 +
    346 +            if not PROCESS_STEP_ID_PATTERN.fullmatch(process_step_id):
    347 +                self.alignment_errors.append(f"Invalid process_step_id: {process_step_id!r}")
    348 +            if process_step_id in seen_step_ids:
    349 +                self.alignment_errors.append(f"Duplicate process_step_id: {process_step_id}")
    350 +            seen_step_ids.add(process_step_id)
    351 +            if not MODULE_ID_PATTERN.fullmatch(module_id):
    352 +                self.alignment_errors.append(f"Invalid process_step_catalog.module_id: {modul
         e_id!r}")
    353 +            if not module_symbol:
    354 +                self.alignment_errors.append(f"Process step {process_step_id} has blank modul
         e_symbol")
    355 +
    356 +            yaml_step = yaml_steps.get(step_number)
    357 +            id_step = id_steps_by_number.get(step_number)
    358 +            if yaml_step is None or id_step is None:
    359 +                self.alignment_errors.append(f"Step {step_number} missing from YAML or identi
         fier_map")
    360 +                continue
    361 +
    362 +            expected_symbol = LOOP_SENTINEL_REMAP.get(str(yaml_step.get("module_id", "")), st
         r(yaml_step.get("module_id", "")))
    363 +            expected_id = str(id_step.get("module_id", ""))
    364 +            if step.get("step_name") != yaml_step.get("name"):
    365 +                self.alignment_errors.append(
    366 +                    f"Step {step_number} name mismatch: catalog={step.get('step_name')!r} yam
         l={yaml_step.get('name')!r}"
    367 +                )
    368 +            if module_symbol != expected_symbol:
    369 +                self.alignment_errors.append(
    370 +                    f"Step {step_number} module_symbol mismatch: catalog={module_symbol!r} ya
         ml={expected_symbol!r}"
    371 +                )
    372 +            if module_id != expected_id:
    373 +                self.alignment_errors.append(
    374 +                    f"Step {step_number} module_id mismatch: catalog={module_id!r} identifier
         _map={expected_id!r}"
    375 +                )
    376 +
    377 +        if process_source_path:
    378 +            self.info.append(f"Process catalog matches YAML source {process_source_path.name}
         ")

    380 +    def _validate_file_registry(
    381 +        self,

    389 +        print("-" * 80)

    431 +            directory_id = row.get("directory_id", "")
    432 +            file_name = row.get("file_name", "")
    433 +            extension = row.get("extension", "")
    434 +            module_id = row.get("module_id", "")

    438 +            file_scope_class = row.get("file_scope_class", "")
    439 +

         th}: {file_id!r}")

    443 +            if not directory_id:
    444 +                self.readiness_errors.append(f"Blank directory_id for {relative_path}")
    445 +            elif not DIRECTORY_ID_PATTERN.fullmatch(directory_id):

         ve_path}: {directory_id!r}")

    448 +                self.alignment_errors.append(f"file_registry relative_path is not normalized:
          {relative_path!r}")
    449 +            if file_name != PurePosixPath(relative_path).name:
    450 +                self.alignment_errors.append(

    452 +                )
    453 +            if extension != PurePosixPath(file_name).suffix:

         _path}: {extension!r}")

    458 +                )

          {last_verified_utc!r}")
    461 +
    462 +            if module_id:

         ow {relative_path}")
    469 +            else:

    474 +                    )
